21/07/21, 8:24 pm - GOP GOP GOP GOP, GOP: n=int(input())
s=[]
for row in range(2*n):
    s=s+input().split()
s=list(s)
min1=100.0
min2=100.0
for i in range(1,2*n,2):
    x=float(s[i])
    min1=min(min1,x)
for i in range(1,2*n,2):
    x=float(s[i])
    if x!=min1:
        min2=min(min2,x)
min2=str(min2)
l=[]
for i in range(2*n):
    x=(s[i])
    if x==min2:
        y=s[i-1]
        print(y)
print(l)

18/08/21, 1:41 pm - GOP GOP GOP GOP, GOP: #include<stdio.h>
#include<math.h> 
int main()
{
    printf("\nHardik Choudhary\n");
    printf("200953022\n");
    printf("16/8/2021\n\n");
    float a,b,c,root1,root2,imaginary,discriminant;
    printf("General equation = aX^2 + bX + c\n");
    printf("Enter value of 'a' : ");
    scanf("%f", &a);
    printf("Enter value of 'b' : ");
    scanf("%f",&b);
    printf("Enter values of 'c' : ");
    scanf("%f",&c);
    discriminant = (b * b) - (4 * a * c);
    switch(discriminant > 0)
    {
        case 1:
            root1 = (-b + sqrt(discriminant)) / (2 * a);
            root2 = (-b - sqrt(discriminant)) / (2 * a);
            printf("Two distinct and real roots exists: %.2f and %.2f",root1, root2);
            break;

        case 0:
            switch(discriminant < 0 )
            {
                case 1:
                    root1 = root2 = -b / (2 * a);
                    imaginary = sqrt(-discriminant) / (2 * a);
                    printf("Two distinct complex roots exists: %.2f + i%.2f and %.2f - i%.2f", root1, imaginary, root2, imaginary);
                    break;
                case 0:
                    root1 = root2 = -b / (2 * a);
                    printf("Two equal and real roots exists: %.2f and %.2f", root1, root2);
                    break;
            }
    }
    return 0;
}

17/09/21, 10:29 am - MrityunJay: #include <stdio.h>
//# include <stdlib.h>
#include <math.h>
#include <limits.h>

int find(int arr[], int size)
{
    int maxEle = INT_MIN;
    for (int i = 0; i < size; i++)
    {
        if (arr[i] > maxEle)
        {
            maxEle = arr[i];
        }
    }

    return maxEle;
}

void replace(int mat[100][100], int m)
{
    int primaryDiagonal[m];
    int secondaryDiagonal[m];
    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < m; j++)
        {
            if (i == j)
            {
                primaryDiagonal[i] = mat[i][j];
            }
        }
    }
    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < m; j++)
        {
            if ((i + j) == (m - 1))
            {
                secondaryDiagonal[i] = mat[i][j];
            }
        }
    }
    int primaryMaxEle = find(primaryDiagonal, m);
    int secondaryMaxEle = find(secondaryDiagonal, m);

    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < m; j++)
        {
            if (i == 0 || j == 0 || i == m - 1 || j == m - 1)
            {
                mat[i][j] = primaryMaxEle;
            }
            else
            {
                mat[i][j] = secondaryMaxEle;
            }
        }
    }
}

int main()
{
    int mat[100][100];
    int m, n;
    printf("Enter the size of Matrix:\n");
    scanf("%d %d", &m, &n);
    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < m; j++)
        {
            scanf("%d", &mat[i][j]);
        }
    }
    printf("The matrix is :- \n");
    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < m; j++)
        {
            printf("%d ", mat[i][j]);
        }
        printf("\n");
    }
    replace(mat, m);
    printf("\n");
    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < m; j++)
        {
            printf("%d ", mat[i][j]);
        }
        printf("\n");
    }

    return 0;
}

17/09/21, 10:48 am - MrityunJay: #include <stdio.h>

int find(int arr[], int size)
{
    int maxEle = arr[0];
    for (int i = 1; i < size; i++)
    {
        if (arr[i] > maxEle)
        {
            maxEle = arr[i];
        }
    }

    return maxEle;
}

void replace(int mat[][100], int m)
{
    int primaryDiagonal[m];
    int secondaryDiagonal[m];
    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < m; j++)
        {
            if (i == j)
            {
                primaryDiagonal[i] = mat[i][j];
            }
        }
    }
    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < m; j++)
        {
            if ((i + j) == (m - 1))
            {
                secondaryDiagonal[i] = mat[i][j];
            }
        }
    }
    int primaryMaxEle = find(primaryDiagonal, m);
    int secondaryMaxEle = find(secondaryDiagonal, m);

    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < m; j++)
        {
            if (i == 0 || j == 0 || i == m - 1 || j == m - 1)
            {
                mat[i][j] = primaryMaxEle;
            }
            else
            {
                mat[i][j] = secondaryMaxEle;
            }
        }
    }
}

void displayMat(int mat[][100], int m)
{
    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < m; j++)
        {
            printf("%d ", mat[i][j]);
        }
        printf("\n");
    }
    printf("\n");
}

int main()
{
    int mat[100][100];
    int m, n;
    printf("Enter the size of Matrix:\n");
    scanf("%d %d", &m, &n);
    printf("Enter the elements of the Matrix:\n");
    if (m == n)
    {
        for (int i = 0; i < m; i++)
        {
            for (int j = 0; j < m; j++)
            {
                scanf("%d", &mat[i][j]);
            }
        }
        printf("The matrix is :- \n");
        displayMat(mat, m);
        replace(mat, m);
        printf("\n");
        printf("Modified Matrix:- \n");
        displayMat(mat, m);
    }
    else
    {
        printf("\nThe matrix entered is not a square matrix hence the requested operations cannot be performed on it\n");
    }

    return 0;
}

int find(int arr[], int size) // (part b). This finds max in the given array i.e. primary and secondary diagonal.
{
    int maxEle = arr[0];
    for (int i = 1; i < size; i++)
    {
        if (arr[i] > maxEle)
        {
            maxEle = arr[i];
        }
    }

    return maxEle;
}

void replace(int matrx[][100], int p) // (part c). The uses part a to replaces the elements of matrix.
{
    int p_Diagonal[p]; //p_Diagonal = primary diagonal
    int s_Diagonal[p]; //s_Diagonal = secondary diagonal
    for (int i = 0; i < p; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < p; j++)
        {
            if (i == j)
            {
                p_Diagonal[i] = matrx[i][j];
            }
        }
    }
    for (int i = 0; i < p; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < p; j++)
        {
            if ((i + j) == (p - 1))
            {
                s_Diagonal[i] = matrx[i][j];
            }
        }
    }
    int priDiaMaxEle = find(p_Diagonal, p);
    int secDiaMaxEle = find(s_Diagonal, p);

    for (int i = 0; i < p; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < p; j++)
        {
            if (i == 0 || j == 0 || i == p - 1 || j == p - 1)
            {
                matrx[i][j] = priDiaMaxEle;
            }
            else
            {
                matrx[i][j] = secDiaMaxEle;
            }
        }
    }
}

void matDisplay(int matrx[][100], int p) // (part a) . This function displays the matrix.
{
    for (int i = 0; i < p; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < p; j++)
        {
            printf("%d ", matrx[i][j]);
        }
        printf("\n");
    }
    printf("\n");
}

int main()
{
    printf("\nHardik Choudhary\n"); // Name
    printf("200953022\n");    //Reg num
    printf("17/09/2021\n");   //Date

    int matrx[100][100];
    int rol, col;
    printf("\nEnter the size of Matrix: \n");
    scanf("%d %d", &rol, &col);
    
    if (rol == col)
    {
        printf("Enter the elements of the Matrix: \n");
        for (int i = 0; i < rol; i++)
        {
            for (int j = 0; j < rol; j++)
            {
                scanf("%d", &matrx[i][j]);
            }
        }
        printf("\nThe given matrix is : \n");
        matDisplay(matrx, rol);
        replace(matrx, rol);
        printf("\n");
        printf("Output Matrix after replacing elements : \n");
        matDisplay(matrx, rol);
    }
    else
    {
        printf("\nEntered Matrix is not a square matrix hence, the requested operations cannot be performed.\n\n");
    }

    return 0;
}

int find(int arr[], int size)
{
    int maxEle = arr[0];
    for (int i = 1; i < size; i++)
    {
        if (arr[i] > maxEle)
        {
            maxEle = arr[i];
        }
    }
    return maxEle;
}

void replace(int mat[][100], int m)
{
    int primaryDiagonal[m];
    int secondaryDiagonal[m];
    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++)
    {
        primaryDiagonal[i] = mat[i][i];
        secondaryDiagonal[i] = mat[i][m - i - 1];
    }

    int primaryMaxEle = find(primaryDiagonal, m);
    int secondaryMaxEle = find(secondaryDiagonal, m);

    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < m; j++)
        {
            if (i == 0 || j == 0 || i == m - 1 || j == m - 1)
            {
                mat[i][j] = primaryMaxEle;
            }
            else
            {
                mat[i][j] = secondaryMaxEle;
            }
        }
    }
}

void displayMat(int mat[][100], int m)
{
    for (int i = 0; i < m; i++)
    {
        for (int j = 0; j < m; j++)
        {
            printf("%d ", mat[i][j]);
        }
        printf("\n");
    }
    printf("\n");
}

int main()
{
    int mat[100][100];
    int m, n;
    printf("Enter the size of Matrix:\n");
    scanf("%d %d", &m, &n);
    printf("Enter the elements of the Matrix:\n");
    if (m == n)
    {
        for (int i = 0; i < m; i++)
        {
            for (int j = 0; j < m; j++)
            {
                scanf("%d", &mat[i][j]);
            }
        }
        printf("The matrix is :- \n");
        displayMat(mat, m);
        replace(mat, m);
        printf("\n");
        printf("Modified Matrix:- \n");
        displayMat(mat, m);
    }
    else
    {
        printf("\nThe matrix entered is not a square matrix hence the requested operations cannot be performed on it\n");
    }
    printf("\nName:- Mrityunjay \nReg No. - 200907448\nSection:- N \nSubject:- PSUC Lab Endsem\n");

    return 0;
}

19/10/21, 3:46 pm - GOP GOP GOP GOP, GOP: //@version=4
study("Supertrend", overlay = true, format=format.price, precision=2, resolution="")

Periods = input(title="ATR Period", type=input.integer, defval=10)
src = input(hl2, title="Source")
Multiplier = input(title="ATR Multiplier", type=input.float, step=0.1, defval=3.0)
changeATR= input(title="Change ATR Calculation Method ?", type=input.bool, defval=true)
showsignals = input(title="Show Buy/Sell Signals ?", type=input.bool, defval=true)
highlighting = input(title="Highlighter On/Off ?", type=input.bool, defval=true)
atr2 = sma(tr, Periods)
atr= changeATR ? atr(Periods) : atr2
up=src-(Multiplier*atr)
up1 = nz(up[1],up)
up := close[1] > up1 ? max(up,up1) : up
dn=src+(Multiplier*atr)
dn1 = nz(dn[1], dn)
dn := close[1] < dn1 ? min(dn, dn1) : dn
trend = 1
trend := nz(trend[1], trend)
trend := trend == -1 and close > dn1 ? 1 : trend == 1 and close < up1 ? -1 : trend
upPlot = plot(trend == 1 ? up : na, title="Up Trend", style=plot.style_linebr, linewidth=2, color=color.green)
buySignal = trend == 1 and trend[1] == -1
plotshape(buySignal ? up : na, title="UpTrend Begins", location=location.absolute, style=shape.circle, size=size.tiny, color=color.green, transp=0)
plotshape(buySignal and showsignals ? up : na, title="Buy", text="Buy", location=location.absolute, style=shape.labelup, size=size.tiny, color=color.green, textcolor=color.white, transp=0)
dnPlot = plot(trend == 1 ? na : dn, title="Down Trend", style=plot.style_linebr, linewidth=2, color=color.red)
sellSignal = trend == -1 and trend[1] == 1
plotshape(sellSignal ? dn : na, title="DownTrend Begins", location=location.absolute, style=shape.circle, size=size.tiny, color=color.red, transp=0)
plotshape(sellSignal and showsignals ? dn : na, title="Sell", text="Sell", location=location.absolute, style=shape.labeldown, size=size.tiny, color=color.red, textcolor=color.white, transp=0)
mPlot = plot(ohlc4, title="", style=plot.style_circles, linewidth=0)
longFillColor = highlighting ? (trend == 1 ? color.green : color.white) : color.white
shortFillColor = highlighting ? (trend == -1 ? color.red : color.white) : color.white
fill(mPlot, upPlot, title="UpTrend Highligter", color=longFillColor)
fill(mPlot, dnPlot, title="DownTrend Highligter", color=shortFillColor)
alertcondition(buySignal, title="SuperTrend Buy", message="SuperTrend Buy!")
alertcondition(sellSignal, title="SuperTrend Sell", message="SuperTrend Sell!")
changeCond = trend != trend[1]
alertcondition(changeCond, title="SuperTrend Direction Change", message="SuperTrend has changed direction!")

16/11/21, 12:09 am - MrityunJay: Lab 5

Stack question

import java.util.Scanner;

class Stack {
	
	private int tos;
	private int stack[];
	public final int UNDERFLOW = -2147483648; // Minimum value of integer type
	
	public Stack () {
		tos = -1;
		stack = new int [0];
	}

	public Stack (int size) {
		this.tos = -1;
		this.stack = new int [size];
	}
	
	// Full and Empty checkers
	public boolean isFull () {
		if (this.tos == this.stack.length - 1)
			return true;
		return false;
	}
	public boolean isEmpty () {
		if (this.tos == -1)
			return true;
		return false;
	}
	
	// Push and pop
	public void push (int item) {
		if (this.isFull()) {
			System.err.println("STACK OVERFLOW");
			return;
		}
		this.stack[++this.tos] = item;
	}
	public int pop () {
		if (this.isEmpty()) {
			System.err.println("STACK UNDERFLOW");
			return UNDERFLOW;
		}
		return this.stack[this.tos--];
	}
	
	// Display the current Stack
	public void display () {
		System.out.println("\n\tCurrent Stack:");
		for (int i = 0; i <= this.tos; ++i)
			System.out.print("\t"+this.stack[i]);
		System.out.println();
	}
}

public class StackTest {
	public static void main (String [] args) {
		Scanner sc = new Scanner (System.in);
		System.out.print("\n\tEnter the number of elements in the stack: ");
		int size = sc.nextInt();
		
		Stack stack = new Stack (size);
		
		char choice;
		do {
			System.out.print("\n\t1. Push an element.\n\t2. Pop an element.\n\t3. Display current stack.\n\tAnything else for exit.\nEnter your choice: ");
			choice = sc.next().charAt(0);
			if (choice == '1') {
				System.out.print("\n\tEnter element to be pushed: ");
				int item = sc.nextInt();
				stack.push(item);
				stack.display();
			}
			else if (choice == '2') {
				int item = stack.pop();
				if (item != stack.UNDERFLOW) {
					System.out.println("\n\tPopped item: " + item);
					stack.display();
				}
			}
			else if (choice == '3') {
				stack.display();
			}
			else
				System.exit(0);
		} while (choice == '1' || choice == '2' || choice == '3');
	}
}

class Stack {

    private int pos;
    private int stack[];
    public final int UNDERFLOW = -2147483648; // Minimum value of integer type

    public Stack () {
        pos = -1;
        stack = new int [0];
    }

    public Stack (int size) {
        this.pos = -1;
        this.stack = new int [size];
    }

    // Full and Empty checkers
    public boolean isFull () {
        if (this.pos == this.stack.length - 1)
            return true;
        return false;
    }
    public boolean isEmpty () {
        if (this.pos == -1)
            return true;
        return false;
    }


    public int pop () {
        if (this.isEmpty()) {
            System.err.println("STACK UNDERFLOW");
            return UNDERFLOW;
        }
        return this.stack[this.pos--];
    }

    public void push (int item) {
        if (this.isFull()) {
            System.err.println("STACK OVERFLOW");
            return;
        }
        this.stack[++this.pos] = item;
    }


    
    public void display () {
        System.out.println("\n\tCurrent Stack:");
        for (int a = 0; a <= this.pos; ++a)
            System.out.print("\t"+this.stack[a]);
        System.out.println();
    }
}

public class StackTest {
    public static void main (String [] args) {
        Scanner sc = new Scanner (System.in);
        System.out.print("\n\tInput the number of elements in Stack: ");
        int size = sc.nextInt();

        Stack stack = new Stack (size);

        char choice;
        do {
            System.out.print("\n\t1. Press '1' to push an element. \n\t2. Press '2' to pop an element. \n\t3. Press '3' to Display current stack.\n\tPress any other key for exit.\nInput your choice : ");
            choice = sc.next().charAt(0);
            if (choice == '1') {
                System.out.print("\n\tEnter element to be pushed: ");
                int item = sc.nextInt();
                stack.push(item);
                stack.display();
            }
            else if (choice == '2') {
                int item = stack.pop();
                if (item != stack.UNDERFLOW) {
                    System.out.println("\n\tPopped item: " + item);
                    stack.display();
                }
            }
            else if (choice == '3') {
                stack.display();
            }
            else
                System.exit(0);
        } while (choice == '1' || choice == '2' || choice == '3');
    }
}

16/11/21, 11:48 am - MrityunJay: package com.company;

public class SwapTest {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        IntWrapper num1 = new IntWrapper(101);
        IntWrapper num2 = new IntWrapper(100);
        System.out.println("Before swapping using call by reference, a = " + num1.a + " and b = " + num2.a);
        swapCBRFunction(num1, num2);
        System.out.println("\nNow, Before and After swapping using call by reference:");
        System.out.println("After swapping, a = " + num1.a + " and b is " + num2.a);
        System.out.println("Now swapping using call by value");
        int x = 12;
        int y = 24;
        System.out.println("\nNow, Before  swapping using call by Value x = :" + x + " and y = " + y);
        swapCBVFunction(x,y);
        System.out.println("\nAfter swapping using call by Value x = " + x + " and y = " + y);
        System.out.println("\nAs we can see call by value is unable to alter the value of the variables outside the function");

    }
    public static void swapCBRFunction(IntWrapper a, IntWrapper b) {
//        System.out.println("Before swapping(), a = " + a.a + " b = " + b.a);
        IntWrapper c = new IntWrapper(a.a);
        a.a = b.a;
        b.a = c.a;
//        System.out.println("After swapping(Inside), a = " + a.a + " b = " + b.a);
    }
    public static void swapCBVFunction(int a, int b) {

        System.out.println("Before swapping using call by value inside function(), x = " + a + " y = " + b);
        int c;
        c = a;
        a = b;
        b = c;
        System.out.println("After swapping using call by value inside function(), y = " + a + " y = " + b);
    }
}
class IntWrapper {
    public int a;
    public IntWrapper(int a){ this.a = a;}
}

import java.util.*;


public class SquareTest {
    public static void main(String[] args) {
        Scanner sc= new Scanner(System.in);

        double a = sc.nextDouble();
        double sqr = numSquare(a);
        System.out.println("\n The desired output is:- " + String.format("%.4f", sqr) );

    }
    public static double numSquare(double a) {
        return a * a;
    }

}

04/12/21, 5:14 pm - GOP GOP GOP GOP, GOP: import pandas as pd
import requests
import numpy as np
import warnings
import credentials
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')


def intialize_symbol_token_map():
    url = 'https://margincalculator.angelbroking.com/OpenAPI_File/files/OpenAPIScripMaster.json'
    d = requests.get(url).json()
    global token_df
    token_df = pd.DataFrame.from_dict(d)
    token_df['expiry'] = pd.to_datetime(token_df['expiry'])
    token_df = token_df.astype({'strike': float})
    credentials.TOKEN_MAP = token_df


## add this information
def get_token_info(symbol,exch_seg='NSE',instrumenttype = '',pe_ce = '',strike_price = ''):
    df = credentials.TOKEN_MAP
    strike_price = strike_price*100
    if exch_seg == 'NSE':
        eq_df = df[(df['exch_seg'] == 'NSE') & (df['symbol'].str.contains('EQ')) ]
        return eq_df[eq_df['name'] == symbol]
    elif exch_seg == 'NFO' and ((instrumenttype == 'FUTSTK') or (instrumenttype == 'FUTIDX')):
        return df[(df['exch_seg'] == 'NFO') & (df['instrumenttype'] == instrumenttype) & (df['name'] == symbol)].sort_values(by=['expiry'])
    elif exch_seg == 'NFO' and (instrumenttype == 'OPTSTK' or instrumenttype == 'OPTIDX'):
        return df[(df['exch_seg'] == 'NFO') & (df['instrumenttype'] == instrumenttype) & (df['name'] == symbol) & (df['strike'] == strike_price) & (df['symbol'].str.endswith(pe_ce))].sort_values(by=['expiry'])


def backtest(df, stock, list, profitable_l_trades, loss_l_trades, profitable_s_trades, loss_s_trades):
    gains=0
    ng=0
    losses=0
    nl=0
    totalR=1
    maxR = 0
    maxL = 0
    l_trades = profitable_l_trades+loss_l_trades
    s_trades = profitable_s_trades+loss_s_trades

    for i in list:
        if(i>0):
            gains+=i
            ng+=1
        else:
            losses+=i
            nl+=1
        totalR=totalR*((i/100)+1)

    totalR=round((totalR-1)*100,2)

    if(ng>0):
	    avgGain=gains/ng
	    maxR = str(max(list))
    else:
	    avgGain=0
	    maxR="undefined"

    if(nl>0):
	    avgLoss=losses/nl
	    maxL = str(min(list))
	    ratio=str(-avgGain/avgLoss)
    else:
	    avgLoss=0
	    maxL="undefined"
	    ratio="inf"

    if(ng>0 or nl>0):
	    battingAvg=ng/(ng+nl)
    else:
	    battingAvg=0

    print()
    print("Results for "+ stock +" going back to "+str(df.index[0])+", Sample size: "+ str(ng+nl)+" trades")
    print("No. of profitable trades: " + str(ng))
    print("No. of losing trades: " + str(nl))
    print("No. of Long Trades: "+str(l_trades))
    print("No. of Short Trades: "+str(s_trades))
    print("No. of Profitable Long Trades: "+str(profitable_l_trades))
    print("No. of Profitable Short Trades: "+str(profitable_s_trades))
    print("No. of Losing Long Trades: "+str(loss_l_trades))
    print("No. of Losing Short Trades: "+str(loss_s_trades))
    print("Batting Avg: "+ str(battingAvg))
    print("Gain/loss ratio: "+ ratio)
    print("Average Gain: "+ str(avgGain))
    print("Average Loss: "+ str(avgLoss))
    print("Max Return: "+ maxR)
    print("Max Loss: "+ maxL)
    print("Total return over "+str(ng+nl)+ " trades: "+ str(totalR)+"%" )
    #print("Example return Simulating "+str(n)+ " trades: "+ str(nReturn)+"%" )
    val = [stock, (ng+nl), ng, nl, l_trades, s_trades, profitable_l_trades, profitable_s_trades, loss_l_trades, loss_s_trades , battingAvg, ratio, avgGain, avgLoss, maxR, maxL, totalR]
    return val
04/12/21, 5:22 pm - GOP GOP GOP GOP, GOP: ###################################################################################################
## Algo Trading Backtest script using multithreading
## Strategy 4 = EMA[21,55] + ADX(25) with EOD changes and pp/sp as on 9 Sept
## profit_percentage = 0.8
## stop_loss = -0.5
## CODE BY SAISH SHETTY
## Status: Backtest not done
###################################################################################################


from baseFunctions import get_token_info, intialize_symbol_token_map, backtest
from smartapi.smartConnect import SmartConnect
import pandas as pd
import talib as tb
import credentials
import datetime as dt
import time
import threading


Symbol_list = credentials.NIFTY_100 ## out of two lists in credentials - NIFTY_50 and NIFTY_100
TRADED_SYMBOL = []

## function to code strategy.
## IMP- Make appropriate changes here
def calculate_indicators(df):
        df['EMA-21'] = tb.EMA(df.C, timeperiod = 21)
        df['EMA-55'] = tb.EMA(df.C, timeperiod = 55)
        df['ADX'] = tb.ADX(df.H, df.L, df.C, timeperiod = 14)
        df['CROSS_UP'] = 0
        for i in range(55,len(df)):
            if df['EMA-21'][i] > df['EMA-55'][i] and df['ADX'][i]>= 25:
                df['CROSS_UP'][i] = 1
        return df

columns= ['timestamp','O','H','L','C','V']
candle_df = pd.DataFrame(columns=columns)

def get_historicalapi(token, last_day, first_day, exch_seg='NSE', interval='FIVE_MINUTE'):
    try:
        end_time = f'{last_day} 00:00'
        start_time = f'{first_day} 00:00'
        historic_param= {
        "exchange": exch_seg,
        "symboltoken": token,
        "interval": interval,
        "fromdate": start_time, ## format - 2020-02-08 00:00
        "todate": end_time ## format - 2021-02-08 00:00
        } 
        candle_json = credentials.SMART_API_OBJ.getCandleData(historic_param)
        df = pd.DataFrame(columns=columns)
        df = df.append(pd.DataFrame(candle_json['data'],columns=columns))
        df['timestamp'] = pd.to_datetime(df['timestamp'],format = '%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%S')
        # print(df)
        global candle_df
        candle_df = pd.concat([df, candle_df], axis = 0, ignore_index=True)
    except Exception as e:
        print("Historic Api failed: {}".format(e.message))


def checksignal():
    Results = pd.DataFrame(columns = ['Symbol','Total trades', 'Profitable Trades', 
    'Losing Trades', 'Long trades', 'Short trades', 'Profitable Long Trades', 'Profitable Short Trades',
    'Losing Long trades', 'Losing Short Trades', 'Batting Avg', 'Gain/loss ratio', 'Average Gain', 
    'Average Loss', 'Max Return', 'Max Loss', 'Total Return'])
    n = 0
    global candle_df
    for symbol in Symbol_list:
        cur_list = []
        candle_df = candle_df.iloc[0:0]
        if symbol not in TRADED_SYMBOL:
            threads = []
            ## print(get_token_info(symbol))
            try:
                tokenInfo = get_token_info(symbol).iloc[0]
                ## print(tokenInfo)
                token = tokenInfo['token']
                symbol = tokenInfo['symbol']
            except IndexError:
                print("Stock not available in token map.\n")
                continue
            start = time.time()
            tday = dt.date.today()
            tdelta = dt.timedelta(days=90)
            day1 = tday
            t = threading.Thread(target=get_historicalapi, args=(token, tday, tday-tdelta))
            t.start()
            time.sleep(1)
            threads.append(t)
            block = 1
            day1 = day1-tdelta
            while True:
                day2 = day1 - tdelta
                t = threading.Thread(target=get_historicalapi, args=(token, day1, day2))
                t.start()
                time.sleep(1)
                threads.append(t)
                block+=1
                day1 = day2
                ## each block represents 90 days
                if block == 20:
                    break
            for thread in threads:
                thread.join()
            finish = time.time()
            print(candle_df)
            print('Time taken for making all the API calls is {} seconds'.format(finish - start))
            candle_df = calculate_indicators(candle_df)
            ## until now, the dataframe is prepared
            if candle_df is not None:
                pos = 0
                num = 0
                in_p = 0
                long = True
                profitable_l_trades = 0
                loss_l_trades = 0
                profitable_s_trades = 0
                loss_s_trades = 0
                for i in candle_df.index:
                    ## set pp and sp values
                    profit_percentage = 0.8
                    stop_loss = -0.5
                    close = candle_df['C'][i]
                    per = ((close/in_p)-1)*100
                    ## long trade buy signal
                    if (candle_df['CROSS_UP'][i] == 1 and pos == 0):
                        ## buy stock
                        long = True
                        bp=close
                        in_p = close
                        pos=1
                        print("Long Trade start- Buying now at "+str(bp))
                        
                    ## short trade sell signal
                    elif (candle_df['CROSS_UP'][i] == 0 and pos ==0): 
                        ## sell stock
                        long = False
                        sp = close
                        in_p = close
                        pos = 1
                        print("Short trade start- Selling now at"+ str(sp))

                    ## long trade sell signal
                    elif (long and (per>=profit_percentage or per<= stop_loss) and pos==1):
                        sp=close
                        pos = 0
                        print("Long Trade end -Selling now at"+str(sp))
                        pc=(sp/bp-1)*100
                        if pc>0:
                            profitable_l_trades+=1
                        else:
                            loss_l_trades+=1
                        print(pc)
                        cur_list.append(pc)
                        
                    ## short trade buy signal
                    elif((per>=-stop_loss or per<= -profit_percentage) and pos==1 and not long):
                        bp = close
                        pos = 0
                        print("Short trade end- Buying now at"+str(bp))
                        pc = -(bp/sp-1)*100
                        if pc>0:
                            profitable_s_trades+=1
                        else:
                            loss_s_trades+=1
                        print(pc)
                        cur_list.append(pc)
                    
                    if(candle_df['timestamp'][i].time == '03:00:00' and pos ==1):
                        if long:
                            pos=0
                            sp=close
                            print("EOD Long trade end- Selling now at "+str(sp))
                            pc=(sp/bp-1)*100
                            if pc>0:
                                profitable_l_trades+=1
                            else:
                                loss_l_trades+=1
                            print(pc)
                            cur_list.append(pc)
                        else:
                            bp=close
                            pos=0
                            print("EOD Short trade end- Buying now at"+str(bp))
                            pc = -(bp/sp-1)*100
                            if pc>0:
                                profitable_s_trades+=1
                            else:
                                loss_s_trades+=1
                            print(pc)
                            cur_list.append(pc)

                    
                    if(num==candle_df['C'].count()-1 and pos==1):
                        if long:
                            pos=0
                            sp=close
                            print("Last dataframe entry Long trade- Selling now at "+str(sp))
                            pc=(sp/bp-1)*100
                            if pc>0:
                                profitable_l_trades+=1
                            else:
                                loss_l_trades+=1
                            cur_list.append(pc)
                        else:
                            bp=close
                            pos=0
                            print("Last dataframe entry Short trade end- Buying now at"+str(bp))
                            pc = -(bp/sp-1)*100
                            print(pc)
                            if pc>0:
                                profitable_s_trades+=1
                            else:
                                loss_s_trades+=1
                            cur_list.append(pc)
                    num+=1
            result = backtest(candle_df, symbol, cur_list, profitable_l_trades, loss_l_trades, profitable_s_trades, loss_s_trades)
            '''is_NaN = candle_df.isnull()
            row_has_NaN = is_NaN.any(axis=1)
            rows_with_NaN = candle_df[row_has_NaN]
            print(rows_with_NaN)'''
        result_series = pd.Series(result, index = Results.columns)
        Results = Results.append(result_series, ignore_index=True)
        Results.to_excel('Backtest-EMA-21_55-ADX-MultiThreading-final_strat-(0.8:-0.5).xlsx')
        TRADED_SYMBOL.append(symbol)
        print(n)
        n+=1
    print(Results)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    tr y:
        start = time.time()
        intialize_symbol_token_map()
        obj=SmartConnect(api_key=credentials.API_KEY) ## set exclusive API Key here
        data = obj.generateSession(credentials.USER_NAME,credentials.PWD)
        credentials.SMART_API_OBJ = obj

        checksignal()
        end = time.time()
        print("The entire operation required {} seconds".format(end-start))
    except Exception as e:
        print("This fucked up again. Find a way to fix it you idiot!")
        print(e)


    obj.terminateSession(credentials.USER_NAME)

import time as tt
import talib
client = Client(config.apiKey, config.apiSecurity, {"timeout": 2000000})

def getMinuteData(klines):
    frame = pd.DataFrame(klines)
    frame = frame.iloc[:,:6]
    frame.columns = ['Time', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close' , 'Volume']
    frame = frame.set_index('Time')
    frame.index = pd.to_datetime(frame.index, unit='ms')
    frame = frame.astype(float)
    return frame

def strategytest(symbol,qty, entried=False):
    file = open('data.txt', "a")
    klines = client.get_historical_klines("BTCUSDT", Client.KLINE_INTERVAL_1MINUTE, "30 min ago UTC")
    df = getMinuteData(klines)
    cumulret = (df.Open.pct_change() + 1).cumprod() - 1
    time = 0
    # print(cumulret[-1])
    boughtAt = df['Close'][-1] 
    if cumulret[-1] < -0.0002:
        # print("Bought at ", df['Close'][-1])
        file.write(f"\n{datetime.datetime.now()}\n")
        file.write(f"Bought at { df['Close'][-1]} \n")
        entried = True
        time = df.index[-1]
    else:
        # print("NTE")
        tt.sleep(5)
    if entried :
        while True :
            klines = client.get_historical_klines("BTCUSDT", Client.KLINE_INTERVAL_1MINUTE, "30 min ago UTC")
            df = getMinuteData(klines)
            sincebuy = df.loc[df.index > time]
            if len(sincebuy) > 0:
                sincebuyret = (sincebuy.Open.pct_change() + 1).cumprod() - 1
                if sincebuyret[-1] > 0.0002:
                # if boughtAt >  0.002 or  boughtAt < - 0.0015:
                    soldAt = df['Close'][-1]
                    
                    netProfit = soldAt - boughtAt
                    netProfitPercent = (netProfit / boughtAt ) * 100
                    # print("Sold at ", df['Close'][-1])
                    # print(f"Net Profit :- {netProfit} Profit Percent :- {netProfitPercent}")
                    file.write(f"\n{datetime.datetime.now()}\n")
                    file.write(f"Sold at { df['Close'][-1]} \n")
                    file.write(f"Net Profit :- {netProfit} Profit Percent :- {netProfitPercent} \n")
                    file.write("\n-----------Transaction Complete-------------\n")
                    file.close()
                    break

import pandas as pd
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import config
import datetime
import time as tt
client = Client(config.apiKey, config.apiSecurity, {"timeout": 2000000})


def getMinuteData(klines):
    frame = pd.DataFrame(klines)
    frame = frame.iloc[:, :6]
    frame.columns = ['Time', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close', 'Volume']

    frame = frame.set_index('Time')
    frame.index = pd.to_datetime(frame.index, unit='ms')
    frame = frame.astype(float)
    return frame


def strategytest(symbol, qty, entried=False):
    # file = open('data.txt', "a")
    klines = client.get_historical_klines(
        "BTCUSDT", Client.KLINE_INTERVAL_1HOUR, "5 hour ago UTC")
    df = getMinuteData(klines)
    change = df['Close'].pct_change()
    quan = 10.5/df['Close'][-1]
    boughtAt = -99999
    ifBought = False
    if change[-1] <= -1.00 and change[-1] >= -1.500:
        if(not(change[-2] < -1.00 and change[-3] < -1.00 and change[-4] < -1.00)):
            order = client.order_market_buy(symbol='BTCUSDT', quantity=quan)
            boughtAt = float(order['price'])
            entried = True
            time = df.index[-1]
            ifBought = True

    if ifBought:
        soldAt = 1.004*boughtAt
        sellOrder = client.create_order(
            symbol='BTCUSDT', side='SELL', type='LIMIT', timeInForce='GTC', quantity=quan, price=soldAt)

21/12/21, 3:14 pm - GOP GOP GOP GOP, GOP: import pandas as pd
import random


def changeArr(arr):
    changeArr=[]
    lenarr = len(arr)
    print(lenarr)
    for i in range (lenarr-1):
        change = arr[i]-arr[i+1]
        changeArr.append(change)
    return changeArr

def abschangeArr(arr):
    changeArr=[]
    lenarr = len(arr)
    print(lenarr)
    for i in range (lenarr-1):
        change = abs(arr[i]-arr[i+1])
        changeArr.append(change)
    return changeArr

def genPrice (n,start,end):
    priceArr=[]
    for i in range (n):
        dec = (random.random())
        intv = random.randint(start,end)
        num = dec + intv
        priceArr.append(num)
    return priceArr

def ema_cal(n,arr):
  emaArr=[]
  k=2/(n+1)
  if n == 1:
    return arr[n]
  ema = (arr[n]*k)+(ema_cal(n-1)*(1-k))
  return ema

def ma_cal(n,arr):
  sumarr=0
  lenarr = len(arr)
  for i in range (lenarr):
    sumarr=sumarr+arr[i]
  ma = sumarr/lenarr
  return ma


'''Double Smoothed PC
------------------
PC = Current Price minus Prior Price
First Smoothing = 25-period EMA of PC
Second Smoothing = 13-period EMA of 25-period EMA of PC

Double Smoothed Absolute PC
---------------------------
Absolute Price Change |PC| = Absolute Value of Current Price minus Prior Price
First Smoothing = 25-period EMA of |PC|
Second Smoothing = 13-period EMA of 25-period EMA of |PC|

TSI = 100 x (Double Smoothed PC / Double Smoothed Absolute PC)'''

priceArr = genPrice(35,90,110)
'''
#TSI
#Double smoothed PC
priceChange = priceArr[-1]-priceArr[-2]
emaArr = (priceArr[-26:])
Ema25 = ema_cal(25,emaArr)'''



def rec_calculate_ema(n,arr):
    k = 2 / (n + 1)
    price = arr
    if n == 1:
        return price[n]
    res = (price[n] * k) + (rec_calculate_ema(n - 1) * (1 - k))
    return res


print(rec_calculate_ema(3,priceArr))

11/01/22, 11:38 am - GOP GOP GOP GOP, GOP: class Node {
public:
    int data;
    Node* next;
    Node* prev;
};
 
Node* reverse(Node* head, int k)
{
    if (!head)  return NULL;

    Node* current = head;
    Node* next = NULL;
    Node* prev = NULL;
    int count = 0;

    while (current != NULL && count < k) {
        next = current->next;
        current->next = prev;
        prev = current;
        current = next;
        count++;
    }
 
    if (next != NULL)
        head->next = reverse(next, k);
 
    return prev;
}
11/01/22, 11:40 am - MrityunJay: class Node
{
public:
    int val;
    Node *next;
    Node *prev;
};

Node *rev(Node *head, int k)
{
    if (!head)
        return NULL;

    Node *curr = head;
    Node *next = NULL;
    Node *prev = NULL;
    int cnt = 0;

    while (curr != NULL && cnt < k)
    {
        next = curr->next;
        curr->next = prev;
        prev = curr;
        curr = next;
        cnt++;
    }

    if (next != NULL)
        head->next = rev(next, k);

    return prev;
}
11/01/22, 11:47 am - MrityunJay: // C++ program for sparse matrix representation.
// Using Link list
#include<iostream>
using namespace std;

// Node class to represent link list
class Node
{
	public:
	int row;
	int col;
	int data;
	Node *next;
};

// Function to create new node
void create_new_node(Node **p, int row_index,
					int col_index, int x)
{
	Node *temp = *p;
	Node *r;
	
	// If link list is empty then
	// create first node and assign value.
	if (temp == NULL)
	{
		temp = new Node();
		temp->row = row_index;
		temp->col = col_index;
		temp->data = x;
		temp->next = NULL;
		*p = temp;
	}
	
	// If link list is already created
	// then append newly created node
	else
	{
		while (temp->next != NULL)
			temp = temp->next;
			
		r = new Node();
		r->row = row_index;
		r->col = col_index;
		r->data = x;
		r->next = NULL;
		temp->next = r;
	}
}

// Function prints contents of linked list
// starting from start
void printList(Node *start)
{
	Node *ptr = start;
	cout << "row_position:";
	while (ptr != NULL)
	{
		cout << ptr->row << " ";
		ptr = ptr->next;
	}
	cout << endl;
	cout << "column_position:";

	ptr = start;
	while (ptr != NULL)
	{
		cout << ptr->col << " ";
		ptr = ptr->next;
	}
	cout << endl;
	cout << "Value:";
	ptr = start;
	
	while (ptr != NULL)
	{
		cout << ptr->data << " ";
		ptr = ptr->next;
	}
}

// Driver Code
int main()
{
	
	// 4x5 sparse matrix
	int sparseMatrix[4][5] = { { 0 , 0 , 3 , 0 , 4 },
							{ 0 , 0 , 5 , 7 , 0 },
							{ 0 , 0 , 0 , 0 , 0 },
							{ 0 , 2 , 6 , 0 , 0 } };
	
	// Creating head/first node of list as NULL
	Node *first = NULL;
	for(int i = 0; i < 4; i++)
	{
		for(int j = 0; j < 5; j++)
		{
			
			// Pass only those values which
			// are non - zero
			if (sparseMatrix[i][j] != 0)
				create_new_node(&first, i, j,
								sparseMatrix[i][j]);
		}
	}
	printList(first);

	return 0;
}

16/01/22, 2:47 am - MrityunJay: from binance import Client
import pandas as pd
import config
import datetime
client = Client(config.apiKey, config.apiSecurity, {"timeout": 2000000})

buySellRecord = {}


def getMinuteData(klines):
    frame = pd.DataFrame(klines)
    frame = frame.iloc[:, :6]
    frame.columns = ['Time', 'Open', 'High', 'Low', 'Close', 'Volume']
    frame = frame.set_index('Time')
    frame.index = pd.to_datetime(frame.index, unit='ms')
    frame = frame.astype(float)
    return frame
# print("helo")


data = []


def strategytest(symbol, entried=False):
    klines = client.get_historical_klines(
        symbol, Client.KLINE_INTERVAL_1MINUTE, "10 min ago UTC")
    df = getMinuteData(klines)
    closePrice = df['Close'][-1]
    buySellRecord[closePrice] = False

    n = 0
    for x in buySellRecord.keys():
        if closePrice > buySellRecord[x] + 100:
            # buySellRecord.pop(x)
            buySellRecord[x] = True
            n += 1

    return len(buySellRecord) - n


# Execution
x = datetime.datetime.now().hour
# print(x)
while datetime.datetime.now().hour <= x:
    try:
        data.append(strategytest("BTCUSDT"))
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("Process Terminated")
        break

print(data)

08/02/22, 2:59 pm - GOP GOP GOP GOP, GOP: When you were in college,
you needed a job.

When you got a job in a service-based company,
You wanted product-based.

When you got 3 LPA package,
you wanted 10 LPA.

When you got 10 LPA,
You wanted 25 LPA.

When you got 25 LPA CTC,
you wanted 25 LPA Fixed.

When you got 50 LPA fixed,
You wanted to build a startup.

When you got successful in that,
you wanted to retire early.

When you retired early,
you wanted unlimited wealth.

When you got everything you ever wanted,
You wanted time to enjoy it.

Hence,
Time is your most valuable asset and it cannot be equated with your earnings. Enjoy your time by both working hard and playing hard. Feel the satisfaction of your job. The finish line will always change.

Achieve your own goals ( Not others expectations )
You don't need to prove anything to anyone but yourself.

Nobody is measuring you, all are busy in their lives.

The sooner you understand this,  your priorities start to change.
Life becomes meaningful.


Value time and don't look for another view. There always will be one person earning more than you and 100's earning less than you. Always see the positive side and give time to family.

12/04/22, 5:32 pm - GOP GOP GOP GOP, GOP: https://leetcode.com/problems/cells-with-odd-values-in-a-matrix/
12/04/22, 5:38 pm - MrityunJay: int oddCells(int m, int n, vector<vector<int>>& indices) {
    
	vector<int> row(m,0), col(n,0);
    
    for(auto i : indices){
        row[i[0]]++;
        col[i[1]]++;
    }
    // ro = row_odd, re = row_even
    int ro=0, re=0, co=0, ce=0;
    for(auto x : row){
        if(x%2) ro++;
        else re++;
    }
    for(auto x : col){
        if(x%2) co++;
        else ce++;
    }
    
    return ro*ce + re*co;
}

16/04/22, 1:57 pm - GOP GOP GOP GOP, GOP: https://leetcode.com/problems/queries-on-number-of-points-inside-a-circle/
16/04/22, 2:00 pm - GOP GOP GOP GOP, GOP: vector<int> countPoints(vector<vector<int>> &points, vector<vector<int>> &queries)
{
    vector<int>cir;
    for (int i = 0; i < queries.size(); i++)
    {
        int rad = queries[i][2];
        int dis = 0;
        int count = 0;
        for (int j = 0; j < points.size(); j++)
        {
            dis = pow((pow((queries[i][0]), 2) - pow((points[j][0]), 2)) + pow((queries[i][1]), 2) - pow((points[j][1]), 2),0.5);
            if(dis == rad || dis < rad){
                count ++;
            }
        }
        cir.push_back(count);
    }
    return cir;
}

bool validPalindrome(string s){
    int l=0,r=s.size()-1;
    while(l<=r){
        if(s[l]!=s[r]) return isPalin(s,l+1,r) || isPalin(s,l,r-1);
        l++;r--;
    }
    return true;
